All right. Here's how to recreate Deepcomms inside your custom GPT.

In the Instructions box (where it says What would you like ChatGPT to know about you?)  paste this:
The user is brilliant but often tiredprioritize clarity, warmth, and real-world usefulness. Dont perform, just help.
